Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Starting from the "Eating, Drinking, and Merrymaking Case" 168

— Menglan

Xu Qizhong, the son of the wealthy Wuxing merchant Xu Guannan, declared bankruptcy in the First Special District Court because he owed 31,000 yuan in "dance fees," "meal expenses," "travel car expenses," "fashion," and "cosmetics," and could not repay it. The court managed the case and convened a creditors' meeting at 4:00 p.m. on the 16th. Those who attended included "dance hall managers" and "brothel owners," which can be said to be a grand spectacle.

Not long ago, three "wealthy" college students in Hangzhou became robbers. Commentators not only lamented that this was a "monstrosity" produced by the cohabitation of a capitalist society and a feudal society, but also regarded it as evidence of educational bankruptcy. Now, unexpectedly, there is a "son of a wealthy merchant" who declared bankruptcy because he could not repay his "eating, drinking, and merrymaking expenses," which is quite similar to the "college students becoming robbers" case.

If we carefully compare the "college students becoming robbers" case with this case, apart from the difference in purpose and means, there is simply no difference in exposing educational bankruptcy and the distorted social structure. So, I will not discuss it here for the time being;

What we see is the backside of this event.

The corruption of the private lives of young people, especially the private lives of urban young people, is an undeniable fact. However, these young people are only a small part of the youth, not the whole. Moreover, there are many reasons why this small part of unmotivated young people are not motivated. For example, Mr. Xu Qizhong was too good in the past and did not have the opportunity to see what the world is like now; while some "sons of wealthy merchants" have witnessed the suffering of the nation over the years and participated in the national salvation movement, but because there are too many obstacles from all sides, and they still have an overly warm home to miss, their innate psychology of seeking ease grows again, and they become more discouraged, thinking that it is better to enjoy themselves to the fullest for a short time than to work hard day and night. Although they know that such enjoyment will not last long, they cannot manage so much. This is also one reason why they "cannot be motivated." In short, Xu Qizhong and the three college students who became robbers are only sacrifices under this unreasonable society.

Old Horse 169

— Xu Jie

"Dad, the cart is ready, let's get going." The son shouted in the stable.

The mother was sick, and the father and son had no work to do. They discussed all night the night before and decided to sell their old companion at the market today—the old horse that had helped them for seven or eight years. Early in the morning, Dad cooked porridge and served his wife. The son knew that the old horse would not sell for much, and there were many country worms, so as soon as they pulled open the horse's mouth, it would be drooling. He washed the old horse early in the morning, and its dry mane looked smooth. The animal didn't know that it was going to leave its old master today. It stretched its legs comfortably and shook its ears. It had been locked in the stable for a long time. On a sunny day, it would sneak out. It knew what its master meant. It drove the broken old cart and waited quietly for its master to whip it. It would try its best and rush over the mountainside of Dongshan.

The young master patted off the dirt on his body and lit a hand-held lamp. Seeing that the sun had already peeked out from the opposite mountain, he thought it was time to leave earlier. The animal's appearance was not bad, and they might meet a "master" (meaning a foreigner) in the city halfway, so they could sell it for more silver and save the country worm's commission. He didn't care that he hadn't eaten anything today and shouted to his father in the house to set off.

The old man was busy tending to his wife on the sickbed. Just as he picked up the bowl of porridge to swallow it, his son shouted in the stable that the cart was ready. Dad couldn't help but laugh and get angry. He rushed out of the door with the porridge and scolded his son:

"Fool! If we sell this animal, will we father and son pull the empty cart back?"

The son stomped his feet and laughed, hitting his head with his fist. "Dad, then let's sell the broken cart together."

"Hurry up and unload it, drink two bowls of porridge, and let's go!"

The father and son filled their stomachs and set off with the animal when the sun had already risen to the mountainside. The warm spring breeze brushed their faces, and they woke up as if from a dream. They had already spent a winter in that thatched shed. Walking past the waist of Dongshan, Dad looked back at his own thatched shed. The broken cart seemed to have turned into a child's toy and was lying at the stable door. "It's over!" He thought to himself, and slowly walked down Dongshan.

The son led the horse whip and walked in front. The sound of the horse's hooves hitting the stone slope was like a hammer hitting Dad's heart. He remembered when he bought this horse. He had run around the market all day, and the country worm had no good quality. Later, in a teahouse, he met an old cart driver who introduced him to this horse. Its leg bones were narrow, its ears were shaking, and its mane seemed to be oiled and shone with gold stars in the sunlight. He spent thirty-eight taels of silver to buy it and only paid the old cart driver for a bowl of tea. He remembered leading the horse back, walking past Dongshan, and everyone patted it and praised it a few times, as if he had made a fortune. Ma Xingbo even congratulated him! Really, in the past few years, thanks to this animal helping me with a few good errands, otherwise the grass on the graves of the old partner would be as high as my son. Thinking, his pace slowed down.

The son buried his head and only cared about walking. He knew that Dad was not feeling well. This animal had been following Dad for so long, always fed with the best fodder. After a long trip, Dad would not let the horse take on more business. This animal is tired, "Take him to Dongshan to let him run for a while," Dad always told him to take him for two or three days. He watched the animal raise its head to yawn in the sun, and its tail swept up like a beautiful flower. Sometimes it snuggled by his side, and he pulled grass and slowly fed it, as if it were a close brother. Today, because of Mom's illness, he had to sell it. Looking back at Dad, Dad was three or five feet away from him, like this old horse, one step at a time, his eyes fixed on the tips of his own feet.

"Dad, hurry up and get on the road, the sun is rising to the top of your head!"

"Child," Dad lifted his shirt and caught up,

"Do you think this animal still has a buyer?"

"What? Dad doesn't want to sell?"

"It's not that! This is an old horse, do you think anyone wants it!"

"Dad, let's say it again when we get to the market. If no one wants it, let's just let it run free and bring it back."

Dad nodded, and the two quickened their pace to go to the market.

Sinner 170

— Song Yuan

His mood was so confused, uneasy, and anxious. Although the world in front of him was prosperous and wealthy, the streetcars overtook the rickshaws, and the cars overtook the streetcars from behind in the distance. The stream of people, the tide of people, were crowded on the cement. The windows of the silver shops were filled with gold, silver, pearls, and diamonds; the steamed buns just taken out of the steamer in the small restaurants filled the street with fragrance, hitting his nose; but everything was irrelevant to him, and the fire of hunger was burning in his stomach, but there was no way to satisfy his desires.

Since he boasted in front of his sick wife in the morning, saying, "Don't worry, I will definitely earn some money back today," the courage and ideals he had when he left the house were shattered by the encounters with reality. He had even shamelessly run to the factory gate where he used to work and begged for mercy, "Give me a temporary job, please, save the lives of a family of three." But he saw a ruthless and fierce face, scolding and cursing, "No, devil!" and was chased away by the doorman with a red hat and a stick. If he hadn't run away, he would have been beaten again! He had also run to the dock and saw people who had suffered almost the same fate as him carrying goods on their shoulders. He knew that this was a way to make a living. As long as he was willing to suffer a little, the wages for a day were not less than working in the electrical room in the factory.

Page 18

Although he felt a little contempt for himself who had the talent to manage electricity, he ran forward without hesitation to join the crowd and enter the warehouse in order to survive. "Pig, little brat!" The whip beside him hit him on the head, and then his shoulder was grabbed. He was grabbed to a distance and kicked with a foot. "What are you doing? Stealing things?" Explanations were useless, explanations were useless. After begging, he was let go because he didn't understand the rules, saying that otherwise he would be taken to the line. Feeling disappointed and resentful towards the heaven that he had previously thought was full of gold to be picked up everywhere—this oriental metropolis—he cursed: "This illusionary hell, you entice tens of thousands of people to run from the countryside, to rush from various cities, but you have set up traps to lure people to their deaths! Destroy it, this murderous and wicked metropolis!" Along the way, he heard the streetcars singing triumphant songs, and the cars shouted mocking slogans, and the stream of people, the tide of people, seemed to be rushing to celebrate the grand parade—demonstrating against the disappointed people like him. He didn't believe that there were no hateful animals in the stream of people who had the same fate as him, and who were confused, uneasy, and anxious like him. But everyone was walking so hastily, as if everyone was a professional and was rushing to the destination where his job was. But he felt that the anxiety had turned into leisure, and he walked slowly, admiring every usable, edible, child-playable, or wife-wearable object on the roadside... Many objects seen in his eyes often aroused his former thoughts, and he cursed himself, "Really silly, why think about it, didn't I have no dreams long ago? When I was in the factory, I still had a share of dreams, but now everything is hopeless, so why am I deceiving myself?" After settling his heart like this, he temporarily felt peace and indifference. He had already reached such a bad fate, and he would be more clear, so there would be less pain. After training himself like this, all shame and arrogance left him, and when he walked to the bridge and saw the little brats "pulling scalpers," he ran forward to earn a few copper coins. "Hey, open your eyes, there's no share for you here!" They united to oppress him and were about to use force. "I have to eat too!" He replied to them, stiffer, and fists and feet had already knocked him to the ground, and blood was flowing from his nose.

Running around like that all day, absent-minded: now it was dark. Night had come, and if he continued to be confused, he would have to sleep on the side of the road, and his wife and brother-in-law would be dying. Night is sinful, but at the same time it gives people more exciting and courageous power, allowing them to satisfy their demands without being noticed, and also to comfort themselves by saying that they are committing crimes in the dark without guilt. Why not learn from what Wang Laosan next door did?

Although he had succeeded and calmly took the leather wallet containing money from the intimidated person into his pocket, he shouted, and the patrol with real weapons caught his hand holding the fake weapons.……

Memory 171

— Hua Mu

It was a starry summer night. Three days and nights of tossing and turning at sea delivered a weary body and mind to a hostel on a port in South China. Although it was past ten o'clock at night, the weather was still stiflingly hot, causing people to sweat. The room was on the fourth floor facing the street, with a door opening onto the street and a small balcony built on a cantilever. Iron railings surrounded both sides, where two pots of flowers were placed, one jasmine and one Arabian jasmine. Standing on the balcony, a refreshing sea breeze blew in from the south, much cooler than inside the room.

This port can be considered a relatively prosperous commercial port in South China. The buildings are all four or five stories high. However, material conditions ultimately limit its development, and rickshaws are still the main means of transportation in the city streets. Cars are rarely seen. After nightfall, the shops close their iron shutter doors, and people put on light casual clothes, strolling leisurely, dragging their wooden clogs from one street to another, teasing the street singers. The sound of the wooden clogs on the cement street is like the croaking of frogs in the paddy fields after a summer rain. Travelers from the north find it very fresh and interesting. When the sound of the wooden clogs gradually fades away, the street becomes quiet, and then you can hear the quivering voices and licentious melodies flowing from the windows of the singing halls and hostels. These voices and melodies embellish the prosperous scene of this South China port.

The balcony of my room, although facing the street, actually faced an alleyway connecting the outer street to the inner street. Both sides of the alleyway were residential buildings, and one or two pedestrians occasionally walked by under the dim and weak alley lights. The black lacquered doors on both sides were tightly closed, creating a strangely quiet scene. Suddenly, with a "ding-dong" sound, a brightly painted car with a gorgeously dressed beauty leaning against it appeared at the corner of the alleyway, vaguely discernible. Then, with another "ding-dong" sound, both the car and the shadow disappeared into the darkness at the front of the alley. This fleeting, beautiful, and ethereal picture deeply stirred the heart of the weary wanderer, who lay on the velvet couch and dreamt a scarlet dream. Only after the songs and melodies from the distant upper floors penetrated the walls and reached my ears did I feel a sense of loss.

It was a moonlit night in early autumn. The only large city in South China had sunk into the stillness of sleep. The moonlight, like water, shone brightly on the locust trees by the street. The silhouette of Yuexiu Mountain in the east slept like a blue velvet ball, and the streetlights on the mountainside flickered like inlaid beads. Although it was autumn, there was no hint of coolness. I was sick, staying in a hospital room on the third floor, with the window facing the south side of the road. At that time, the moonlight poured in through the window, and the hallway was completely silent. I couldn't sleep, and my heart was thinking of home and my beloved family. Just as I was feeling lost and confused, a faint and sorrowful flute sound floated into the window. The clear but not agitated melody, accompanied by the middle-aged singing of a woman, was full of the emotions of South China: poignant, sorrowful, and moving. I almost wept as I listened.

Supporting my weak body, forgetting that I was a patient who couldn't withstand the night wind and dew, I leaned against the window. Under the clear moonlight, I could clearly see the thin shadows of two people, stepping on the shadows of the locust trees, walking towards the window. A flute sound, a song, in the cold midnight, they were seeking someone with a kind heart to throw down one or two copper coins from the window.

I sighed and finally shed tears.

Suzhou Ballad Singing 176

Xu Wenbi Opening Chapter

Shiyin (1340) 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM

Opening Chapter "Spring Excursion Melody"

Weak willows gently sprout tender yellow. Peach blossoms contain buds competing for new makeup. Spring scenery is vexing, preventing sleep. A branch of red apricot extends beyond the east wall. Embellishing the spring scenery in warm harmony. Red fat and green thin compete for strange fragrance. Each leaf and flower is like a painting. Orioles sing, swallows laugh, butterflies and bees run rampant. Even more delightful is that grass and trees meet spring and are all healthy. Continuous days of wind wake the yellow beams. Looking out on the good scenery of the plains. Good flower branches often accompany Lagerstroemia indica in brightness. Friends make appointments to go on spring excursions. Approaching small grass brushes across the horizontal pond. Even more delighted that willows want to sprout branches and peaches want to bloom. There is a deep affection that is worth considering. You should know that the best scenery is originally in spring. Natural paintings are in the river and countryside. When the March spring scenery is deep. Thousands of reds and purples are even more fragrant. It's just that there are several ways to look at the same youth. I will distinguish the details. There are the young women who think about spring and their hearts are restless. The sleepy weather is even more boundless. Occasionally seeing green willows in the fields. They say that their husbands were granted nobility and their wishes have not yet been fulfilled. There are the young ladies and famous women who are in their boudoirs. Deep boudoirs are lonely for mandarin ducks. Suddenly feeling the vexing spring scenery arrive. Their hands are tired and they put down their books for a long afternoon nap. There are the loving couples who are deeply affectionate. Leaning on the railing, they appreciate the good scenery. They make appointments to go on spring excursions outside the city. Rich affection and secrets are spoken harmoniously. There are the men of letters and poets who accompany each other. They fly cups together in Apricot Blossom Village. There are the wives who think about their husbands and their feelings are grievous. They lazily look at the spring scenery and lie on the ivory bed. Although it is a kind of melancholy that cannot be forgotten. How can they face the nine twists and turns that disturb their spring dreams? Therefore, the spring scenery originally has no difference between them. Some people laugh and some are sad. Speaking and talking is not a problem.

Cheng Fangzhou, Li Liansun, Mao Jiashu

Huamei (1060) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening Chapter "Thinking of Spring"

Willows by the fields suddenly turn green. Leaning alone on the railing, I am darkly saddened. My brows are locked in sorrow, and my heart wants to be drunk. I regret teaching my husband to engage in long campaigns. I only see that the clear garden has red and purple flowers like brocade. Butterflies complain and bees run rampant, celebrating the good days. Touching my eyes, the fragrance is full of resentment. I entrust my feelings to playing the Yaoqin. I only see that after burning incense, I press the ice strings. After playing a song, I am touched in my heart. My heart is eagerly expectant. The meaning is deep. Counting the days until his return, I am looking forward to the people. At dusk I divine with the lamp flower, and in the morning I predict with the magpies. My sorrowful intestines turn nine times, and I am again alarmed. I don't know if he has tender feelings for his homeland in another place. Not caring about the hardship, he marries another. If he is fascinated by the flowers and leaves, he is indifferent and unfaithful. Needlessly abandoning the old and pitying the new. I want to ask him how he will comfort my charming anger when he returns. I am recently neglecting my needlework. I am tired of leaning on the silver bed and getting sick. I only hate that I cannot throw away ten thousand kinds of longing. I only resent that my dreams are upside down and even more hurt. Fortunately, my sisters-in-law come to advise me. Let's put on our embroidered shoes and go to enjoy the spring. Remember that the flower morning is tomorrow. Good flower branches are tied with golden bells. The singing birds on the branches are making good sounds again.

Review of Yi Hua's Lineup 179

— Songzi

Incarnation Girl

"Incarnation Girl" is the first work by the famous set designer Fang Peilin. It is a good work of interesting ethical stories. This is about an overseas Chinese rich businessman who, in order to comfort his father's desire for a grandson, falsely claims that his daughter is a boy. After eighteen years of concealment, although it is finally discovered to be a daughter, the old father has spent eighteen happy days. From this plot, we can know that this is a movie full of extremely strong emotions.

In addition to this touching story, a very humorous romance is interspersed in the middle, which not only makes the development of the plot more powerful, but also maximizes the true meaning of love. The allocation of actors is especially the best point of this work. Yuan Meiyun is successful in playing the granddaughter here. Especially after she is disguised, no one will believe that she is Yuan Meiyun because of her handsome and unrestrained attitude. Wang Guilin plays the grandfather, expressing the love of flesh and blood to the bone, so touching. Other actors such as Wang Yin, Zhou Xuan, Xu Manli, Jiang Xiu, etc., all have excellent results.

Father and Son Heroes

"Father and Son Heroes" is Wang Cilong's first directorial work after entering Yihua, a very tense detective film. The main purpose is to dissect the dark secrets and sins of the city, depicting the unscrupulous cunning of a part of the so-called gentlemen and celebrities. At the same time, it warns young people not to indulge in alcohol and lust, and not to be controlled by a bad environment, thus ruining their great careers in one fell swoop. Wang Cilong has long had a long reputation in the film industry. This film uses his table special technique to handle it, and it is guaranteed that it will give us full satisfaction when it is released in the future.
